2019-01-27 10:32:15,765 [32] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService.GetBinCheckDataInfo
SELECT B.PACKAGE_GUID,B.BIN_NO,B.CREATION_DATE,D.MATER_NO,D.MATER_NAME,D.PALLET_NO,D.BATCH_NO,D.PRODUCT_QTY,D.PRODUCT_DATE,P.MEMO,
	      (CASE WHEN D.CHECK_STATUS=0 THEN　'待检'　WHEN　D.CHECK_STATUS=1 THEN '合格' ELSE '不合格'  END) CHECK_STATUS
        FROM WBS_PACKAGE_DATA D inner join WBS_BIN B on B.PACKAGE_GUID=D.PACKAGE_GUID 
		    LEFT JOIN PSB_PRODUCT P ON P.PRODUCT_GUID=D.PRODUCT_GUID
		    WHERE D.MATER_NO <> 'BPALLET'
        
        ORDER BY B.creation_date

2019-01-27 11:01:43,899 [48] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@InOutBinHistory
SELECT T.BIN_GUID,
        T.BIN_NO,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN '入库'
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN '出库'
        END IO_TYPE,
        T.CREATION_DATE,
        T.PALLET_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NO,T2.MATER_NO) MATER_NO,
        ISNULL(T1.MATER_NAME,T2.MATER_NAME) MATER_NAME,
        CASE WHEN T.FINISH_FLAG IS NULL OR T.FINISH_FLAG = '_' THEN '正常'
        ELSE T.FINISH_FLAG END FINISH_FLAG,
        CASE WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'I' THEN ISNULL(T3.SLOC_NO,T4.SLOC_NO)
             WHEN T.IO_TYPE = 'O' THEN ISNULL(T3.ELOC_NO,T4.ELOC_NO) 
        END LOC_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_NO,T4.TASK_NO) TASK_NO,
        ISNULL(T3.CREATION_DATE,T4.CREATION_DATE) CREATE_TASK_DATE,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_START_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_START_DT) TASK_EXEC_START_DT,
        ISNULL(T3.TASK_EXEC_END_DT,T4.TASK_EXEC_END_DT) TASK_EXEC_END_DT
        FROM Z50_WBS_BIN T
        LEFT JOIN WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T1 ON T1.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_PACKAGE_DATA T2 ON T2.PACKAGE_GUID = T.PACKAGE_GUID
        LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK T3 ON T3.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
        LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK T4 ON T4.TASK_GUID = T.TASK_GUID
       where   T.CREATION_DATE >= @param0    AND  T.CREATION_DATE <= 1+ @param1
参数：
@param0=2019/1/22 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/27 0:00:00

2019-01-27 11:36:24,958 [46] DEBUG IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService [(null)] - IEMS.Frame.DbCI.McUIService.Select@CrnErrLog
SELECT T.*, T1.ERR_NAME,
                ISNULL(WT.PALLET_NO,ZWT.PALLET_NO) AS PALLET_NO,
                ISNULL(WT.SLOC_NO,ZWT.SLOC_NO) AS SLOC_NO,
                ISNULL(WT.ELOC_NO,ZWT.ELOC_NO) AS ELOC_NO
          FROM Z40_CRN_FORK_ERR_LOG T
          LEFT JOIN PSB_CRN_ERR T1
            ON T.ERR_NO = T1.ERR_NO
          LEFT JOIN WBS_TASK WT
            ON WT.TASK_NO = T.TASK_NO
          LEFT JOIN Z50_WBS_TASK ZWT
            ON ZWT.TASK_NO = T.TASK_NO
       WHERE   T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME >= @param0    AND  T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME <=1+  @param1    
         ORDER BY T.ERR_BEGIN_TIME desc
参数：
@param0=2019/1/27 0:00:00
@param1=2019/1/27 0:00:00

SELECT B.PACKAGE_GUID,B.BIN_NO,B.CREATION_DATE,D.MATER_NO,D.MATER_NAME,D.PALLET_NO,D.BATCH_NO,D.PRODUCT_QTY,D.PRODUCT_DATE,P.MEMO,
	      (CASE WHEN D.CHECK_STATUS=0 THEN　'待检'　WHEN　D.CHECK_STATUS=1 THEN '合格' ELSE '不合格'  END) CHECK_STATUS
        FROM WBS_PACKAGE_DATA D inner join WBS_BIN B on B.PACKAGE_GUID=D.PACKAGE_GUID 
		    LEFT JOIN PSB_PRODUCT P ON P.PRODUCT_GUID=D.PRODUCT_GUID
		    WHERE D.MATER_NO <> 'BPALLET'
        
        ORDER BY B.creation_date

2019-01-27 15:49:53,446 [75] DEBUG IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService [(null)] - IEMS.JHWMS.DbCI.BinDataService.GetBinCheckDataInfo
SELECT B.PACKAGE_GUID,B.BIN_NO,B.CREATION_DATE,D.MATER_NO,D.MATER_NAME,D.PALLET_NO,D.BATCH_NO,D.PRODUCT_QTY,D.PRODUCT_DATE,P.MEMO,
	      (CASE WHEN D.CHECK_STATUS=0 THEN　'待检'　WHEN　D.CHECK_STATUS=1 THEN '合格' ELSE '不合格'  END) CHECK_STATUS
        FROM WBS_PACKAGE_DATA D inner join WBS_BIN B on B.PACKAGE_GUID=D.PACKAGE_GUID 
		    LEFT JOIN PSB_PRODUCT P ON P.PRODUCT_GUID=D.PRODUCT_GUID
		    WHERE D.MATER_NO <> 'BPALLET'
        
        ORDER BY B.creation_date
